Texturina Medium Regular (Texturina[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Texturina' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Texturina Medium'.

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '

NID 6 is 'Texturina-MediumItalic', Everything looks good.

Texturina Medium Italic (Texturina-Italic[opsz,wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Texturina' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium Italic' = NID 1 'Texturina Medium' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.
